ACTOR ItThatDistortsTruthItThatDistortsTruth : ItThatDistortsTruthNS3
{
  Tag "It, that Distorts Truth"
  DropItem "None"
  Health 3500
  +INVULNERABLE
  +NOPAIN
  Obituary "%o was left an empty, mindless shell by It, that Distorts Truth."
  var int user_angle;
  States
  {
  Spawn:
	SILE A 0
	SILE A 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.05)
	SILE AAAABBBBB 2 A_FadeIn(0.05)
  Idle:
    SILE AB 10 A_Look
    Loop
  See:
	SILE A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("SpellcardActive",1,"ChaseState")
    SILE G 10 Bright A_FaceTarget
    SILE H 8 Bright A_FaceTarget
    SILE IJKLMN 4 Bright A_FaceTarget
  SpellcardDeclareLoop:
	SILE A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("EnemyCounter1", 180, "SpellcardDeclareFinish")
	SILE A 0 A_GiveInventory("EnemyCounter1", 1)
	SILE A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_angle", user_angle+2)
	SILE A 0 A_CustomMissile("FakeVileFireSpawnerFaster", 32, 0, user_angle)
	Loop
  SpellcardDeclareFinish:
	TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("EnemyCounter1",200)
	TNT1 A 0 Thing_ChangeTID(0,6228)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartAttack",0,6228,2,true)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartTimer",0,6228,80)
	SILE A 0 ACS_Execute(602,0,118)
	SILE A 0 A_GiveInventory("EnemyCounter2",random(1,4))
	SILE A 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/spellcard",0,1.0,0,ATTN_NONE)
	SILE A 0 A_GiveInventory("SpellcardActive",1)
	SILE A 0 A_UnSetInvulnerable
	TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
    SILE O 8 Bright A_FaceTarget
    SILE P 20 Bright
    Goto See
  ChaseState:
	SILE A 0 A_Jump(32,"Teleport")
	SILE A 0 A_SetTranslucent(0.50)
    SILE AABBCCDDEEFF 2 A_Chase
    Loop
  Missile:
    SILE G 10 Bright A_FaceTarget
    SILE H 8 Bright A_FaceTarget
    SILE IJKLMN 4 Bright A_FaceTarget
	SILE N 0 A_TakeInventory("EnemyCounter1", 200)
  MissileLoop:
	SILE A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("EnemyCounter1", 90, "MissileContinue")
	SILE A 0 A_GiveInventory("EnemyCounter1", 1)
	SILE A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_angle", user_angle+4)
	SILE A 0 A_CustomMissile("FakeVileFireSpawner", 32, 0, user_angle)
	Loop
  MissileContinue:
	TNT1 N 0 A_TakeInventory("EnemyCounter1", 200)
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("EnemyCounter2",4,"Missile4")
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("EnemyCounter2",3,"Missile3")
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("EnemyCounter2",2,"Missile2")
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("EnemyCounter2",1,"Missile1")
	Goto Missile1
  Missile1:
	SILE A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("EasyMode",1,"Missile1Easy")
	SILE A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("NormalMode",1,"Missile1Normal")
	SILE A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("HardMode",1,"Missile1Hard")
	SILE A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("LunaticMode",1,"Missile1Lunatic")
	Goto Missile1Lunatic
  Missile1End:
	SILE P 0 A_TakeInventory("EnemyCounter1", 200)
	SILE P 20 A_FaceTarget
	Goto See
  Missile1Easy:
	SILE O 8 A_FaceTarget
	SILE A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_angle", random(0,10))
  Missile1EasyLoop:
	SILE A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("EnemyCounter1", 36, "Missile1End")
	SILE A 0 A_GiveInventory("EnemyCounter1", 1)
	SILE A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_angle", user_angle+10)
	SILE A 0 A_CustomMissile("ItThatDistortsTruthFireballSpeed8", 32, 0, user_angle)
	Loop
  Missile1Normal:
	SILE O 8 A_FaceTarget
	SILE A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_angle", random(0,8))
  Missile1NormalLoop:
	SILE A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("EnemyCounter1", 45, "Missile1End")
	SILE A 0 A_GiveInventory("EnemyCounter1", 1)
	SILE A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_angle", user_angle+8)
	SILE A 0 A_CustomMissile("ItThatDistortsTruthFireballSpeed8", 32, 0, user_angle)
	Loop

ACTOR ItThatDistortsTruthItThatSetsEternityAblaze : ItThatDistortsTruthNS3
{
  Health 4000
  Speed 16
  FastSpeed 24
  +INVULNERABLE
  +NOPAIN
  Tag "It, that Sets Eternity Ablaze"
  Obituary "%o was turned to ash by It, that Sets Eternity Ablaze."
  var int user_angle;
  SeeSound ""
  PainSound "Monster/diapai"
  DeathSound "Monster/diadth"
  ActiveSound "Monster/diaact"
  DropItem "None"
  States
  {
  Spawn:
	SILE A 0
	SILE A 2 A_SetTranslucent(0.05)
	SILE AAAABBBBB 2 A_FadeIn(0.05)
  Idle:
    SILE A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("SpellcardActive",1,"Idle2")
    SILE AB 10 A_Look
    Loop
  Idle2:
    DIAB AB 10 A_Look
    Loop
  Pain:
    DIAB Q 5
    DIAB Q 5 A_Pain
    Goto See
  See:
	SILE A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("SpellcardActive",1,"ChaseState")
    SILE G 0 Bright A_FaceTarget
    SILE G 10 Bright A_FaceTarget
    SILE H 8 Bright A_FaceTarget
    SILE IJKLMN 4 Bright A_FaceTarget
	TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("EnemyCounter1", 200)
	TNT1 A 0 Thing_ChangeTID(0,6229)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartAttack",0,6229,0,true)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartTimer",0,6229,90)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_angle", 0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("EnemyCounter2",random(1,4))
	DIAB A 0 A_SetTranslucent(1.0)
	DIAB A 0 ACS_Execute(602,0,119)
	DIAB A 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/spellcard",0,1.0,0,ATTN_NONE)
	DIAB A 0 A_PlaySound("Monster/diasit",0,1.0,0,ATTN_NONE)
	DIAB A 0 A_GiveInventory("SpellcardActive",1)
  DeclareSpellLoop1:
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("EnemyCounter1", 18, "DeclareSpell2")
	TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("EnemyCounter1", 1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_angle", user_angle + 20)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("DiabolistFireEffect", sin(user_angle) * 64, cos(user_angle) * 64, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0)
	Loop

	DIAB O 3 Bright A_FaceTarget

  Missile4Lunatic:
